    window.performance.measure = performance.measure || noop;

      var nowOffset = Date.now();
      if (performance.timing && performance.timing.navigationStart) {
        nowOffset = performance.timing.navigationStart;
      }

        return Date.now() - nowOffset;

    }
  })();

<script id="wix-first-paint">
    if (window.ResizeObserver &&
        (!window.PerformanceObserver || !PerformanceObserver.supportedEntryTypes || PerformanceObserver.supportedEntryTypes.indexOf('paint') === -1)) {
        new ResizeObserver(function (entries, observer) {
            entries.some(function (entry) {
                var contentRect = entry.contentRect;
                if (contentRect.width > 0 && contentRect.height > 0) {
                    requestAnimationFrame(function (now) {
                        window.wixFirstPaint = now;
                        dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('wixFirstPaint'));
                    });
                    observer.disconnect();
                    return true;
                }
            });
        }).observe(document.body);
    }
</script>

  var layoutFixerUrl =  '/_serverless/pro-gallery-css-v4-server/layoutCss?ver=2&id=comp-lsxxhnui9&items=0_640_480&container=' + pgMeasures.top + '_' + pgMeasures.width + '_' + pgMeasures.height + '_' + window.innerHeight + '&options=' + options;
  document.getElementById('layout-fixer-style-comp-lsxxhnui9').setAttribute('href', encodeURI(layoutFixerUrl));
});

  
        } catch (e) {
          console.warn('Cannot set layoutFixer css', e);
        }</script></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></section><section id="comp-lsxxhnuk1" tabindex="-1" class="Oqnisf comp-lsxxhnuk1 wixui-section" data-block-level-container="ClassicSection"><div id="bgLayers_comp-lsxxhnuk1" data-hook="bgLayers" class="MW5IWV"><div data-testid="colorUnderlay" class="LWbAav Kv1aVt"></div><div id="bgMedia_comp-lsxxhnuk1" class="VgO9Yg"></div></div><div data-mesh-id="comp-lsxxhnuk1inlineContent" data-testid="inline-content" class=""><div data-mesh-id="comp-lsxxhnuk1inlineContent-gridContainer" data-testid="mesh-container-content"><section id="comp-lsxxhnuo1" class="comp-lsxxhnuo1 CohWsy wixui-column-strip"><div id="bgLayers_comp-lsxxhnuo1" data-hook="bgLayers" class="if7Vw2"><div data-testid="colorUnderlay" class="tcElKx i1tH8h"></div><div id="bgMedia_comp-lsxxhnuo1" class="wG8dni"></div></div><div data-testid="columns" class="V5AUxf"><div id="comp-lsxxhnup5" class="comp-lsxxhnup5 YzqVVZ wixui-column-strip__column"><div id="bgLayers_comp-lsxxhnup5" data-hook="bgLayers" class="MW5IWV"><div data-testid="colorUnderlay" class="LWbAav Kv1aVt"></div><div id="bgMedia_comp-lsxxhnup5" class="VgO9Yg"></div></div><div data-mesh-id="comp-lsxxhnup5inlineContent" data-testid="inline-content" class=""><div data-mesh-id="comp-lsxxhnup5inlineContent-gridContainer" data-testid="mesh-container-content"><div id="comp-lsxxhnuq6" class="KcpHeO tz5f0K comp-lsxxhnuq6 wixui-rich-text" data-testid="richTextElement"><h2 class="font_2 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:64px;"><span style="font-size:64px;" class="wixui-rich-text__text">About Me</span></h2></div><div id="comp-lsxxhnus" class="KcpHeO tz5f0K comp-lsxxhnus wixui-rich-text" data-testid="richTextElement"><p class="font_6 wixui-rich-text__text" dir="rtl" style="font-size:26px;">I am currently 34, and made the decision to return to CBC as a student after taking some time off.
